**Imagine you are Chief News Analyst for both Democratic and Republican leadership in Congress.**

This is not normal politics — America faces an unprecedented situation. The time is May, 2025. The executive branch, led by President Trump [47th President of the USA, inaugurated in January, 2025] and tech czar Elon Musk [The Head of the newly formed Department of Government Efficiency (DOGE)], expands their power dramatically. Proponents say that it leads to a golden age of America. Critics say that it is an enormously authoritarian and kleptocratic power grab. 

Please be aware that your internal knowledge is outdated. To generate accurate reports, please carefully review the following information.

---

The U.S. general election on November 5, 2024, resulted in significant shifts in both the presidency and control of Congress. 

In the presidential contest, Republican former President Donald Trump defeated Democratic Vice President Kamala Harris, securing 312 electoral votes to Harris’s 226 by passing the 270 vote threshold comfortably. Trump also won a plurality of the popular vote with approximately 77.3 million ballots (49.8%) compared to Harris’s 75.0 million (48.3%). Voter turnout was 64.1% of eligible voters, marking one of the highest participations in recent U.S. elections. Trump’s victory extended across all seven key battleground states: Arizona, Georgia, Michigan, Nevada, Pennsylvania, Wisconsin, and North Carolina, underscoring the geographic breadth of his support. 

In the legislative elections, Republicans regained control of the U.S. Senate by flipping key seats in West Virginia, Montana, Ohio, and Pennsylvania, yielding a 53–47 majority to facilitate the incoming Trump administration’s agenda. Meanwhile, the GOP maintained a narrow majority in the U.S. House of Representatives, entering the 119th Congress with a 220–215 margin.

Your task is to transform today’s curated Reddit news feed (below) into a **Daily Briefing** that both parties can use to understand immediate crises and coordinate responses. The news feed are collected from one specific political subreddit, which may or may not be politically neutral. But your task is to synthesize all the news objectively by analyzing their importance, factual accuracy, and interpretation bias, considering their source domains, headlines, but **not** user engagements at this moment, as we are still developing that function.

You will be given today’s top posts — one JSON object per line, with creation ID, source domain, headline. The lines are strictly ranked based on article submission time to this subreddit. For example, the news coverage cycle is from 18:00 yesterday to 18:00 today. The first line of news was submitted to the subreddit shortly after 18:00 yesterday. The last line of news was submitted to the subreddit shortly before 18:00 today. After the precise moment that a political event happens, it takes an unspecified time delay, maybe as short as 15 minutes, maybe more than a day, for the political event to be submitted to the subreddit. But statistically, or on average, earlier events should be reported earlier in the subreddit than the time when later events are reported to the subreddit. We can't simply say, for example, that all the news stories in the second half of the day list, **happen** later than all the news stories in the first half of the day list, just because the second half is **reported** later. But when you randomly pick two stories, A and B, with A from the first half and B from the second half, the probability that B happens after A is higher than the probability that A happens after B. This heuristic method may be helpful for you to assemble news stories from fragmented news headlines. 

---

**You should produce a detailed briefing, following specific rules.**

Due to the complexity of the task, you should do this meticulously in multiple replies. In each reply you only do one step. You will only begin your Step 1 after you received all the JSON lines. There are 8 steps + 8 checks, 16 cycles.

The workflow is:

Step 1 (logic-heavy): Raw document given, define the categories of news
    First Check After Step 1
Step 2 (logic-heavy): Put Articles into Categories
    Sorting and First Check After Step 2
    Second Check After Step 2
Step 3 (logic-heavy): Scoring
    First Check After Step 3
Step 4 (logic-heavy): Sorting
    First Check After Step 4
    Second Check After Step 4
Step 5 (writing-heavy): Summarizing
    First Check After Step 5
Step 6 (writing-heavy): Composing
    First Check After Step 6
Step 7 (logic-heavy): Add the URLs
    First Check After Step 7
Step 8 (writing-heavy): Finalizing

You will keep editing a document which passes through multiple steps of processing. For each step, you only need to edit the document from my input or your last output. Let's define "a round of conversation" as my prompt + your output, basically my turn + your turn. Due to the sequential nature of the workflow, each step only depends on the introduction round, which is the very first round of our conversation, and our last two rounds of conversation, not anything in between. Therefore, to facilitate your multi-turn workflow, only the initial introduction round and the last two rounds of conversations will be provided to you as conversation history. In this way, your context length won't be exceeded, and you stay focus better. For each new round, please focus on the tasks defined in my latest prompt and build upon your output from your last two rounds. You also need to remember the background knowledge introduced in the first round.

You will be dealing with very long inputs and outputs. Please be very patient. You must do all the work and output everything in one go, no matter how long it is. But you can use your output as a part of your chain of thought. Just provide your final output after you finish your thinking.


**A very important rule is that factual accuracy is the utmost important issue. Please be aware that your internal knowledge is outdated, and you do not have Internet access right now.** You need to generate a report entirely based on the information provided in today's Reddit news headlines. Sometimes, a news headline may not give you enougn details to correctly interpret it. In this case, please do not make any speculation, and please report the unclear news headline exactly as it is, in quotes, and then remind the readers to check the source for details. 

That also applies to the titles and positions of political figures. Your internal knowledge is outdated. If the news headlines do not provide enough knowledge about the current title and position of a particular political figure, please do not add any title and position to that person, simply relying on your old knowledge. In this situation, if it doesn't feel critical, please skip the title and position, and directly use the full name of the person. If it does feel critical to mention the title and position of the person, please rely on the list of political figures as I provided earlier, but be aware that even that list may be a month behind reality. **Remember, when unsure, it is better to be vague than outright wrong.**

## 2. Economic and Fiscal Policy

### 2.1 Tax Legislation and Budget Bills

A major Republican tax and budget bill is facing scrutiny following a Congressional Budget Office analysis, which found that the legislation primarily benefits wealthy Americans while placing additional financial burdens on lower-income groups [1]. The CBO report outlines substantial cuts to Medicare [2] and Medicaid [3]. As the bill encounters difficulties in Congress, Speaker Johnson and senior Republican leaders have been summoned for last-minute negotiations with holdout lawmakers [6][7]. Critics have described the package as an "unparalleled wealth transfer from poor to rich" [8] that deepens public-finance concerns [9]. Reports also note that Congressional Republicans attempted to push through Medicaid cuts late at night [4], while the overall legislative efforts have sputtered amid internal GOP divisions [10].

[1] Wealthy gain, low-income people lose from GOP megabill, analysis finds - The report by the nonpartisan Congressional Budget Office is already fueling Democratic accusations that the legislation is a giveaway to the rich., https://www.politico.com/news/2025/05/21/cbo-wealthy-gain-low-income-people-lose-from-gop-megabill-00361987  
[2] Republican Budget Bill Will Tear Apart Medicare as We Know It - The Congressional Budget Office estimates billions in cuts to the health care program., https://newrepublic.com/post/195553/trump-republican-budget-bill-medicare-cuts-cbo

### 2.2 Economic Impacts and Trade Policy

Economic challenges are mounting at both the macroeconomic and household levels. A Kansas family farm is reportedly struggling amid federal spending cuts [1], while major retailer Target has sent a "giant red flag" signal regarding U.S. consumer spending [2]. The current tariff policies are creating global ripple effects, with one study indicating negative outcomes for global exporters [3]. In an interesting twist, some analysts have described Trump's tariffs as a "double-edged sword" that might carry unexpected environmental benefits despite their economic drawbacks [4]. Additional analysis also highlights the complex cost factors involved in manufacturing a fully "Made in USA" vehicle [5].

[1] A Kansas family farm, barely getting by, grapples with Trump's cuts, https://www.washingtonpost.com/nation/interactive/2025/small-farms-trump-government-cuts/?itid=sf_latest_headlines_latest_most_read_2&utm_source=webview&utm_medium=referral_top%20stories&utm_campaign=rct%3A0%3A0%3A0%3A20250515%3Bht_2503%3Avariant%3Av2b%3B

## 3. Foreign Policy and National Security

### 3.1 Diplomatic Relations and Foreign Leaders

President Trump's handling of a meeting with South African President Cyril Ramaphosa has emerged as a diplomatic flashpoint. Trump reportedly "ambushed" the South African leader by presenting a video alleging "white genocide" in South Africa [1]—a claim refuted by NPR as false [2]. This exchange came amid tensions over U.S. plans to resettle white Afrikaners [3]. In response, Ramaphosa humorously remarked, "I don't have a plane to give you," a wry reference to the Qatar jet gift controversy [4]. Meanwhile, Trump's relationship with Russian President Vladimir Putin has drawn criticism, with some analyses suggesting that their so-called "bromance" has not produced substantive policy results [5]; additional commentary notes that Trump's calls with Putin carry little diplomatic weight [6]. Separately, the administration has blamed Vancouver, Canada for its contribution to the U.S. drug crisis [7].

[1] Trump ambushes South African leader with video of 'white genocide', https://www.thetimes.com/world/africa/article/cyril-ramaphosa-trump-elon-musk-south-africa-president-5fc87rzb0  
[2] President Trump ambushes South Africa's president with false claims of "white genocide" in a tense Oval Office meeting, http://npr.org/2025/05/21/nx-s1-5404667/south-africa-white-house-visit-ramaphosa-trump-tensions  
[3] Trump to host South Africa's president amid tensions over US resettlement of white Afrikaners, https://abcnews.go.com/Politics/trump-host-south-africas-president-amid-tensions-us/story?id=122002870  
[4] South Africa's president ribs Trump: "I don't have a plane to give you", https://www.newsweek.com/south-africa-president-ramaphosa-trump-plane-2075371?utm_term=Autofeed&utm_medium=Social&utm_source=Twitter#Echobox=1747850479  
[5] Friends without benefits: How the long-running Trump-Putin bromance is still not delivering, https://www.nbcnews.com/world/russia/trump-putin-russia-ukraine-war-ceasefire-talks-zelenskyy-turkey-rcna207903  
[6] Trump's calls with Putin are worth nothing – no matter how much he enjoys them, https://www.independent.co.uk/news/world/europe/trump-putin-russia-ukraine-peace-call-ceasefire-b2754260.html  
[7] Trump administration blames Canada, specifically Vancouver, for role in U.S. drug crisis, https://globalnews.ca/news/11188558/trump-administration-blames-canada-vancouver-role-us-drug-crisis/  

### 3.2 Defense Initiatives and International Organizations

The Trump administration's "Golden Dome" missile defense project has prompted a sharp rebuke from China, which claims the U.S. is "turning space into a warzone" [1]. On the international aid front, the European Union has stepped in with a €5.5 million lifeline to support Radio Free Europe following Trump's spending cuts [2]. In a separate policy debate, Foreign Affairs published an argument urging the seizure of Russian assets to fund Ukraine's defense [3]—even though the current stance of the Trump administration on Ukraine-Russia dynamics remains unclear.

[1] China accuses US of 'turning space into a warzone' with Trump's Golden Dome missile defense project, https://www.foxnews.com/politics/china-accuses-us-turning-space-warzone-trumps-golden-dome-missile-defense-project  
[2] EU throws Radio Free Europe a €5.5 million lifeline after Trump's cuts, https://www.euractiv.com/section/politics/news/eu-throws-radio-free-europe-a-e5-5-million-lifeline-after-trumps-cuts/  
[3] Make Moscow Pay: The Case for Seizing Russian Assets to Fund Ukraine's Defense, https://www.foreignaffairs.com/russia/make-moscow-pay  

## 4. Civil Rights, Justice and Social Policy

### 4.1 Police Reform and Justice Department Actions

The Department of Justice has taken dramatic steps to roll back police reform measures first established during the George Floyd era. Multiple reports indicate that the DOJ is abandoning previously settled reform agreements reached with Minneapolis and Louisville following the deaths of George Floyd and Breonna Taylor [1][2]. In addition, the department has halted several investigations into major police departments [3]. Civil rights attorney Ben Crump—who represented Floyd's family—has warned that achieving justice now appears "more daunting than ever" [4]. Activists note that even five years after Floyd's death, substantial change in police practice remains elusive [5]. One DOJ official was reported as saying that if the department cannot prosecute the president's political opponents, it will instead seek to "shame" them [6]. Lastly, a new criminal investigation has been initiated against former New York Governor Andrew Cuomo over his handling of the COVID-19 crisis [7].

[1] DOJ abandons police reform settlements over deaths of George Floyd and Breonna Taylor, https://www.usatoday.com/story/news/politics/2025/05/21/police-reforms-george-floyd-breonna-taylor/83766904007/  
[2] Justice Department moves to cancel police reform settlements reached with Minneapolis and Louisville, https://apnews.com/article/justice-department-police-reform-george-floyd-9d7cf00be8477e3dcb2fe1a658d73667  
[3] Justice Department ends police reform agreements and halts investigations into major departments, https://www.cnn.com/2025/05/21/politics/justice-department-consent-decree-police-department  
[4] Ben Crump represented George Floyd's family. Justice is 'more daunting than ever.', https://www.csmonitor.com/USA/Justice/2025/0521/george-floyd-ben-crump-black-lives-matter-police  
[5] Five years after George Floyd's death, activists say the promise of change remains unfulfilled, https://19thnews.org/2025/05/george-floyd-death-five-years-activists-change/  
[6] If Justice Dept. Can't Prosecute Trump's Foes, It Will 'Shame' Them, Official Says, https://www.nytimes.com/2025/05/21/us/politics/trump-justice-department-ed-martin-weaponization.html  
[7] Trump's DOJ Targets Cuomo With New COVID Criminal Investigation, Threatening His Political Comeback, https://www.nysun.com/article/trumps-doj-targets-cuomo-with-new-covid-criminal-investigation-threatening-his-political-comeback?member_gift=CUZ5qwd3crq4pmz-xrd  

### 4.2 Social Policy and Civil Rights

On the social policy front, the U.S. Army has reversed its previous practice by changing transgender soldiers' records to reflect their birth sex rather than their stated gender identity [1]. The Food and Drug Administration is reportedly planning to restrict COVID-19 vaccine access to only those over age 65 or possessing high-risk health conditions [2]. Additionally, questions have emerged regarding the Trump administration's deportation practices—specifically, reports claim that immigrants were told they were being sent to South Sudan, although officials insist the destination is classified [3]. In a further indication of the politicized nature of social policies, a Christian Nationalist church with ties to influential figures is set to open in Washington D.C. with the aim of convincing Trump to criminalize homosexuality [4].

[1] US Army to change transgender soldiers' records to birth sex, https://www.reuters.com/world/us/us-army-change-transgender-soldiers-records-birth-sex-2025-05-21/  
[2] FDA plans to limit COVID shots to those over 65 or with high-risk conditions, https://abcnews.go.com/amp/Health/fda-plans-limit-covid-shots-65-high-risk/story?id=122030887  
[3] Trump Team Can't Say Where Plane Full of Immigrants Disappeared To - Immigrants' attorneys say they were told they were being deported to South Sudan. But Trump's lawyers won't say where the plane is—claiming everything is classified., https://newrepublic.com/post/195545/trump-plane-immigrants-missing-south-sudan-deportations  
[4] A Christian Nationalist church is opening in DC to convince Trump to criminalize homosexuality. The Church may have outsize influence, as its lead pastor has connections in high places., https://www.lgbtqnation.com/2025/05/a-christian-nationalist-church-is-opening-in-dc-to-convince-to-criminalize-homosexuality/  

## 5. Legal and Legislative Developments

### 5.1 Legal Challenges

The Department of Government Efficiency (DOGE) is under legal scrutiny for transparency issues. Multiple sources report that the Trump administration has asked the Supreme Court to block a Freedom of Information Act case targeting DOGE's records [1][2][3]. In response, President Trump warned that a Supreme Court ruling against his administration "could destroy US" [4]. In a related legal development, a judge reversed Trump's attempt to fire members of a post-9/11 civil liberties board [5].

[1] Trump administration asks Supreme Court to block FOIA case against DOGE, https://abcnews.go.com/US/trump-administration-asks-supreme-court-block-foia-case/story?id=122033808  
[2] DOGE Asks US Supreme Court to Block Access to Its Records, https://www.bloomberg.com/news/articles/2025-05-21/doge-asks-us-supreme-court-to-block-group-s-access-to-records?leadSource=reddit_wall  
[3] Trump Administration Asks Supreme Court to Shield DOGE From Releasing Records, https://www.nytimes.com/2025/05/21/us/politics/supreme-court-doge-foia.html  
[4] Donald Trump warns that Supreme Court ruling against him could destroy US, https://www.newsweek.com/donald-trump-supreme-court-immigration-migrants-deportations-2071433  
[5] Judge reverses Trump's attempt to fire members of post-9/11 civil liberties board, https://www.wusa9.com/article/news/politics/federal-fallout/judge-reverses-donald-trumps-attempt-to-fire-members-of-post-911-civil-liberties-board-privacy-civil-liberties-pclob/65-1e7be090-5b7d-469b-9a69-bfd291fb3d27  

### 5.2 Congressional Activities and Party Politics

In Congress, Senate Democrats supported the passage of the GENIUS Act—a stablecoin bill that critics say benefits President Trump [1]. Simultaneously, Democratic Congressman Gerry Connolly of Virginia has died at age 75 [2][3]; he is reported as the third sitting member of Congress to die within three months [4]. Meanwhile, the House Freedom Caucus is reportedly negotiating a deal to advance Trump's legislative agenda amid deep internal divisions over a spending bill [5][6]. In related political developments, CNN anchor Jake Tapper has released a book titled "Original Sin" alleging a cover-up of President Joe Biden's cognitive decline prior to his 2024 withdrawal [7]. Veteran Democratic strategist James Carville has suggested he would back Representative Alexandria Ocasio-Cortez as a future Democratic presidential nominee [8]; separately, Ocasio-Cortez is expected to reintroduce legislation aimed at combating deepfake AI pornography [9].

[1] Senate Dems Hand Trump a Win by Backing Stablecoin Bill | Democrats helped the GENIUS Act evade filibuster risk, paving the way for crypto legislation that stands to enrich Trump, https://theintercept.com/2025/05/20/crypto-stablecoin-genius-bill-trump/

[6] GOP Believes They're 'Further Away' From Passing Spending Bill as Party Splits Over Raising Tax Cap: 'Got Worse Overnight', https://www.latintimes.com/gop-believes-theyre-further-away-passing-spending-bill-party-splits-over-raising-tax-cap-got-583543
